TITLE      Simultaneous Measurement of 235U Fission and Capture   14518  1    3 
           Cross Sections From 0.01 eV to 3 keV Using a Gamma     14518  1    4 
           Multiplicity Detector                                  14518  1    5 
AUTHOR     (Y.Danon,D.Williams,R.Bahran,E.Blain,B.Mcdermott,      14518  1    6 
           D.Barry,G.Leinweber,R.Block,M.Rapp)                    14518  1    7 
INSTITUTE  (1USARPI,1USAKAP)                                      14518  1    8 
REFERENCE  (J,NSE,187,291,2017)                                   14518  1    9 
FACILITY   (LINAC,1USARPI) measurement was conducted at Rensselaer14518  1   10 
           Polytechnic Institute using the electron linear        14518  1   11 
           accelerator at the Gaerttner LINAC Center.             14518  1   12 
DETECTOR   (NAICR)A 16-segment NaI(Tl) gamma-multiplicity         14518  1   13 
           detector located at the 25-m experimental station was  14518  1   14 
           used for the measurement. The overal dimensions of     14518  1   15 
           segmented detector were diameter 30.5 cm and length    14518  1   16 
           30.5 cm. A 5.08-cm-diameter collimated neutron beam    14518  1   17 
           passed into the center of the detector through on-axis 14518  1   18 
           cylindrical hole with diameter of 8.9 cm. There was a  14518  1   19 
           1.0-cm-thick annular B4C liner enriched to 99.5 at. %  14518  1   20 
           in 10B between the central beam path and the NaI(Tl)   14518  1   21 
           segments to minimize low-energy neutrons scattering    14518  1   22 
           from the sample and then interacting with the          14518  1   23 
           detector segments.                                     14518  1   24 
ANALYSIS   Fission and capture reactions were measured            14518  1   25 
           simultaneously using segmented high-efficiency gamma   14518  1   26 
           multiplicity NaI(Tl) detector. The multiplicity of     14518  1   27 
           fission gamas peaks at multiplicity 8 to 10 is higher  14518  1   28 
           than the multiplicity of capture gamma cascade, which  14518  1   29 
           peaks at multiplicity 3 to 4. Total deposited gamma    14518  1   30 
           energy was used to separate fission from capture       14518  1   31 
           reactions. The gamma multiplicity was used to improve  14518  1   32 
           the separation.This method enabled capture and fission 14518  1   33 
           yield measurements up to neutron energy of 3 keV.      14518  1   34 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Total uncertainty, which include               14518  1   35 
                   - counting statistics                          14518  1   36 
                   - normalization values                         14518  1   37 
                   - correction for false capture                 14518  1   38 
            The overal uncertainty is dominated by the            14518  1   39 
            normalization uncertainty                             14518  1   40
